 chhattisgarh main hone vaale dwitiya charan ke chunaav ke liye chunaav ayog ne taiyaari puri kar lee he
 On November 19, 80 thousand employees will vote for 72 assembly seats in 19 districts of the state from 8 am to 5 pm
 in kshetron main 843 ummidavaar bhagya aajamaa rahe hai
 Chhattisgarh Chief Electoral Officer Sunil Kujur said that 80 thousand employees have been deployed for polling
 72 vidhansabha siton main se 46 seat saamaanya varg ke liye 17 ajaja ke liye tathaa 9 aja varg ke liye arakshit hai
 About 1 crore 39 lakh, 75 thousand 470 voters will vote in this phase
 inamen se purush matadaataaon kii sankhya 71,39,631 tathaa mahila matadaataaon kii sankhya 68,30,179 he
 At the same time, the number of service voters included in the security force is 5660
 vidhansabha chunaav 2013 ke liye 75 mahila pratyaashee bhi chunaav maidan main hai
 Of these, 236 are from recognized national parties, 289 from registered political parties and 318 independents
 kujur ne bataaya ki sabase kam pratyaashee saraaipali vidhansabha seat main hai jahaan maatr 5 pratyaashee chunaav maidan main hai
 The maximum number of candidates are contesting from Raipur Nagar South Assembly seat
 yahaan se 38 pratyaashee chunaav maidan main hai
 a 3 BU (ballet Unit) machine will be installed for these
 vahiin shantipurna tathaa nishpaksh chunaav karaane ke liye 72 mukhya tathaa saamaanya abjarwaron ke saath hi police vibhaag se 19 abjarwar tainaat kiye gaye hai
 4675 micro observers have been deployed at each level for monitoring
 gadabadi pakadaney ke liye udandaste kii 216 timen banaai gai hai
 75 teams have been formed for video surveillance
 gadabadi rokane ke liye 3 hajaar video camere upyog kiye ja rahe hai
 As many as 17350 polling stations have been set up for polling in 72 assembly seats, out of which 665 auxiliary polling stations are in place
 is tarah kul matdaan kendron kii sankhya 18015 he
 Kujur said in response to a question that special security arrangements have been made in Naxal-affected districts of the state and all the districts where Naxalite activities have been reported or where there is a possibility of Naxalite movement
 samvedansheel ilaakon main sarguja, mahasamund, gariyaaband, baalod, balrampur, surajpur aadi shaamil hai
 The violent protests in Assam and Tripura against the Citizenship Amendment Bill are affecting traffic
 railway ne assam or tripura aane-jane vaali sabhi yatri trainon ko nilambit kar diya or lambii duuri vaali trainon ko guwahati main hi roka ja rahaa he
 At the same time, the airline indigo has canceled all flights to and from Dibrugarh
 company ne yatriyon ko iske liye alternet flite lene yaa rifund kii peshkash kii he
 Subhanan Chanda, spokesperson of the Northeast Frontier Railway, said that this decision was taken on Wednesday night in view of the security situation, after which many passengers were stranded in Kamakhya and Guwahati
 buudhvaar raat guwahati main anischitkaal ke liye karfu laga diya gaya tha kyonki yahaan pradarshnakariyon ne assam ke mukhyamantri sarbanand sonoval or kendriya mantri rameshwar taili ke ghar ko nishaanaa banaaya tha
 a railway station was set on fire by protesters on Wednesday night at Chabua in Dibrugarh, the hometown of Assam Chief Minister
 iske alaava tinsukiya jile main panitola railway stesan ko bhi aag ke hawaale kar diya gaya
 Director General of RPF Kumar Arun Kumar told pti-bhasha that 12 companies of Railway Protection Special Force (RPSF) have been sent to the area
 piem modi or vitt mantri sitaraman kaa jataayaa shukriyaahira udyog par GST ghataane kaa bhi swaagatmaharashtra vidhansabha chunaav kii taarikh kaa elaan hote hi rajya main raajnneetik sargarmi tej ho gai he
 Maharashtra Chief Minister Devendra Fadnavis spoke to the media on various issues at bjp's state headquarters on Monday
 is maukey par bijepi netaa bhupendra yadav or maharashtra bijepi adhyaksh chandrakant dada patil bhi fadanvis ke saath manch par maujuud the
 The Chief Minister thanked Prime Minister Narendra Modi and Finance Minister Nirmala Sitharaman for the reduction in corporate tax
 fadanvis ne corporate tex main katautee ke faisle ko saahasik kadam bataaya
 He also said that Maharashtra will be one of the states benefiting from it
 corporate tex ghataane se maharashtra ko milegaa labhnenavis ne kaha, â€œchina or america main trade war chal rahaa he
 So many companies are turning to South Asia
 jo companiyaan mejority production ke liye jaani jaati hai, wo bhi bharat aa sakati hai
 Economists were demanding that corporate tax should be reduced to achieve a $ 5 trillion economy
 ham vishwaas karte hai ki ab or companiyaan bharat, khaas taur par maharashtra main aaengi, jise bharat kaa menuphaccharing hub mana jaataa he
 According to Fadnavis, there are many companies that recently came to Maharashtra and invested up to Rs 9000 crore
 mukhyamantri ne kaha ki punarnivesh se kai companiyon ko laabh milegaa or isse rojgaar srujit honge, labhaansh se market ooncha hoga
 Merger of banks good move Fadnavis called the merger of 4 banks with ten banks a good step
 mukhyamantri ne kaha, â€œis kadam se aise bainkon ko madad milegi jo band hone kii kagaar par the
 This will increase their lending capacity, increase profits, reduce losses
 centre sarkaar ne rashtriyakrut bainkon main 70,000 karod rupee daale hai
 With this, the lending capacity of banks has reached 5 lakh crore
 mukhyamantri ne kaha ki repo rate nau saal main sabase nichle str par he
 People are getting the benefit of this which was not there before
 saath hi karj kaa byaaj rate bhi gira he
 Research under Corporate Social Responsibility The Chief Minister said that under Corporate Social Responsibility (CSR), corporates can now also invest in research
 isse zyada uniwarsities ko siesaar fund ke tahat privet companiyon se shodh ke liye paisa mil sakegaa
 In addition, companies will be able to conduct research for their company through universities
 hira udyog par GST ghataane kaa swaagatfdanvis ne kaha ki desh se hira sabase zyada niryaat hota he
 GST on this profession with global competition reduced from 5% to 1

 input bhashaa India bowled the record bowling of Yuzvendra Chahal (25 / 6) to beat England by 75 runs in the third decisive T20 match played in Bangalore to win the three-match series 2-1
 bharat se mili 203 ranon ke chunauteepurn lakshya kaa peechha karne utari england team 16
 Stacked 127 runs in 1 over
 chahal ko 'main of da match' or 'main of siries' donon aword mili
 Chahal took six wickets for 25 runs in his four-over quota
 antarrashtriya tii-20 main yujavendra kisi ek pari main sarvshereshth pradarshan karne vaale gendbaaj ban gaye
 In this case he finished third in the world
 unase aage sirf srilanka ke ajanta mendis hi hai
 Ajanta Mendis has the best bowling record in any one innings in the International T20, which he has done twice
 mendis ne sitambar, 2012 main zimbabwe ke khilaaf aath ran dekar chah wicket liye the
 Earlier in August 2011, Mendis took six wickets for 16 runs against Australia
 match ke baad chahal ne kaha, 'bahut acha lag rahaa he, kyonki rashtriya team kii ore se main pehali baar bangaleru main khel rahaa tha, jo mujhe hameshaa se apane ghar jaisaa laga
 In the IPL, i bowled during the powerplay and Kohli showed confidence in me
 lekin sochaa bhi nahin tha ki chah wicket mil jaaenge
 'it is noteworthy that Chahal has been a part of Royal Challengers Bangalore in IPL, with Kohli as captain
 england ek samay 13 overon main do wicket par 117 ran banaakar majboot sthiti main najar aa rahaa tha
 But in the 14th over, Chahal reversed the match by taking the wickets of Ian Morgan (40) and Joey Root (42) off two consecutive balls
 england ko sam billings ke rup main pehla jhatka aath ke kul score par laga

 haalanki iske baad jesan roy (32) ne root ke saath 9
 a partnership of 47 runs at a run rate of 72 brought his team back on track
root with captain Morgan after jesan roy ke out hone ke baad root ne captain morgan ke saath 8

 lekin chahal ke haathon 14wein over main donon ballebaaj lagaataar do gendon par pavilion laute or iske saath hi england ke haathon se jeet phisal gai
 Root hit four fours and two sixes in 37 balls, while Morgan hit two fours and three sixes in a 21-ball innings

 Apart from Chahal, Jasprit Bumrah played a key role in the victory by taking three wickets
 sansad main vipakshi hamale ke asaar ko lekar hunkaar bharte hue bhaajapa ne sushamaa swaraj, vasundhara raaje or shivaraj singh chouhan jaise apane netaaon par prahaar kaa aakraamak tareeke se jawaab dene tathaa congress netaaon se jude vivaad uthaane kaa faisla kiya
 BJP President Amit Shah held strategic meetings with various party colleagues and party spokespersons including Union Ministers Arun Jaitley, Sushma Swaraj, Smriti Irani, Ravi Shankar Prasad and Piyush Goyal in view of the Monsoon Session of Parliament starting on Tuesday, during which Rajasthan Chief Minister Vasundhara Raje was also present
 iske saath hi, shah ne ranneeti ko or behatar banane ke liye jetali or rajnath singh tathaa venkaiya naidu jaise anya varisht netaaon ke saath pradhanmantri narendra modi se mulaakaat kii
 Chauhan also later reached Delhi to participate in the conversation
 kisi kaa istipha nahin lene kii baat spasht karte hue baithak main yah bhi charchaa hui ki mangalvaar se shuru ho rahe satr ke dauraan sansad main in muddon par vipaksh ke hamale kaa muqabla or sarkaar evam party ke jawaab ko kaise susangat kiya jayega
 The Congress has threatened that Parliament proceedings will not be allowed to run if the demand for Raje, External Affairs Minister Sushma and Madhya Pradesh Chief Minister Chauhan is not accepted

 Know which cities of India were changed
 1
 Panjigova's capital Panaji was formerly known as 'panjim'
 konkani bhashaa main ise 'ponnaje' bhi kaha jaataa he
 The city was ruled by the Portuguese until the 1960s and was later renamed
 teenon naam sanskrit se bane hai or iskaa matlab 'naav' hota he
 2
 banaras ban gaya varanasi1956 kii baat he jab banaras ko badalakar 'varanasi' kar diya gaya
 The name is derived from two rivers named 'varuna' and 'asi' flowing in the city
 rugaved main ise 'kaashi' kaha gaya he
 3
 indhur se indoremadhya pradesh ke is shahar kaa naam maratha shashan ke dauraan 'indhur' rakhaa gaya tha lekin british shashan kaal main ise badalakar 'indore' kar diya gaya
 The city is named after the famous Indreshwar temple here, where Indradev is worshiped
 'indhur' ek marathi naam he
 4
 bombai se mumbaimaharashtra kii rajdhani bombai kaa naam badalakar 1996 main mumbai kar diya gaya tha
 The name was derived from 'mumba' (maha Amba) i
e
 Mumbadevi and 'I', which is called mother in Marathi
 1995 se pehle shiv sena bombai kaa naam badalakar mumbai kiye jane kaa dabaav banaati rahi
 The political party said that the name of Mumbai has been changed to Bombay
 5
 From Ropar, the town of Mohali in Rupnagar, Punjab, was earlier named Ropar but was later renamed Rupnagar
 kaha jaataa he ki shahar kaa naam rupnagar, rokatior naamak raja ne rakhaa tha, jisane 11veen sadi main shashan kiya tha
 Rocheshar named the city Ropar after his son Roop Sen
 6
 Madras became Chennai
 In August 1996, Madras was renamed to Chennai
 tamilnadu sarkaar ne shahar ke naam main badlaav ko manjuuri di
 At that time, the names of many cities of the country were being changed
 sarkaar ne tamil bhashaa or samskruti ko badhaava dene ke liye shahar kaa naam badla tha
 7
 simla se shimlahimachal pradesh kii rajdhani kaa naam british kaal main simla hua karata tha
 It was the summer capital of the British, the summer capital
 angrejon se desh kii aazaadee ke baad iske naam ko bhi aaazaad kar ise shimla kar diya gaya
 8
 baroda hua vadodaragujrat ke shahar baroda kaa naam saal 1974 main badal kar vadodara kiya gaya tha
 Earlier it was also known by the names Virakshetra and Veeravati
 baad main iskaa naam vadodara ho gaya, jo sanskrit shabd vatodar se bana he
 Vatodar means Banyan tree
 vadodara kaa aitihaasik naam vadapdrak bhi he
 Adding to this name in 1974, the city was named Vadodara
 9
 Calcutta Now Kolkata Year Calcutta, the capital of West Bengal, was renamed Kolkata in 2001
 kolkata naam ko kalikata se jod kar dekha jaataa he
 Before the British conquered Bengal, one of the three villages in this region was called Kalikata
 baaki do gaanv kaa naam sutanuti or govindapur the
 The name Kalikata derives from the name of mother Kali
 10
 Pondicherry, now Pondicherry, not a French city, Pondicherry was renamed as Puducherry in 2006
 puducheri ek tamil naam he jiskaa arth hota he nayaa shahar
 11
 mohali se esees nagarmohali kaa naam aupchaarik taur par badalakar guru gobind singh ke bade bete sahibajada ajit singh ke naam par rakh diya gaya
 To save time, it came to be called SAS Nagar
 14 april 2006 ko esees nagar ko ropar or patiala jilon se katkar punjab kaa 18waan jila bana diya gaya tha
 12
 cochin se kochikochi kerala ke ernakulam jile ek bada bandargah shahar he
 It was renamed in the year 1996
 kochi ek malayalam shabd kochu aji se bana he, jiskaa matlab hota he ek choti jhil
 In the 17th century, Italian explorers said that it was named after the river Kochi, which connects the sea to the city
 pehle portugali or phir angrej ise cochin bulaane lage
 However, it was renamed Kochi in 1996
 13
 Trivandrum became Thiruvananthapuram In 1991 the capital of Kerala, Trivandrum was renamed Thiruvananthapuram
 thiru-anant-puram malayalam bhashaa ke shabd hai jiskaa matlab hota he bhagwaan anant kaa shahar
 Lord Anant Dev is worshiped in the famous Sri Padmanabhaswamy Temple in Kerala
 14
 Very few people know that Kaunpur was formerly known as Kaunpur
 jaisaa ki naam se hi mahasoos ho jaataa he ki angrej apni sahuuliyat ke hisaab se ise counpur bulaate or jaisaa wo bolte the, usee naam se use likhaa bhi jane laga
 However, within a year of independence from the British, the name of the city was also freely given and changed its old name to Kanpur
 15
 Pune, Pune, about 150 km from Pune, was originally called Poona but was renamed in 1977
 kaha jaataa he ki angrejon ne 1977 main hi iskaa naam badal diya tha
 According to experts, it was called Pune just for the convenience, while some say that it is named after Punya Giri
